< Review>
Asked them to make the two burgers well done and when I get back to the house, they were literally pink. They're thin patties so not hard to cook to a brown color. I also said seasoning salt on the fries and fhey literally poured the whole bottle on the fries, uneatable.

The two grilled cheeses we're just nasty looking and the guy cooking (wearing the Mexican flag hat) just looks like he has an atittude. He was working right next to the owner and they still had the nerve to throw my food half cooked into the bag.

This place has been around for a long time and maybe it's time to close it down. They can't seem to keep the quality consistent and I just noticed they have a B grade. I've seen dirtier looking places that have a better food grade. All in all, very disappointed and no, I won't be coming back.

Thanks Larry, but no thanks.< /Review>

<date>1567633586672< /date><Rating>5< /Rating><Review>This place is great, with a lot of resources for women in need.
Its a 'day shelter' where you can sit indoors in the heat/ac, charge your phone, get cool water, or use the bathroom. They have a limited amount of spots for using the showers every weekday, so get there early. They serve breakfast every weekday morning until 9am. You can use this as a mailing address and use their phone or get messages. Once a week you can get toiletries like pads, socks, underwear, shampoob tooth paste and other stuff depending on the donations available. You can also get a small amount of diapers, wipes, baby food and formula. Sometimes they even have clothes and camping gear, but again it depends on the donations available. You can also get stamps, I believe its 1 per week. Quiet places to sit and sleep during the day. Its a small space, but theres a play ground outside for kids, and Mustard Seed school for all grades. Loaves & Fishes next door serves lunch every day of the week 11a-1pm, has mens showers and laundry, and has lockers to store stuff in, as well as hosting sac self help housing starting at 9am during the week.<//Review><pics>None<//pics>< Resp>

<user_id>114791409395424308256< /user_id>< Text>
Such a blessing to me. There is no other place like this in California or anywhere else in the whole world that I am aware of. The courageous, compassionate and giving women, volunteers and employees have no idea what anyone is truly dealing with on a regular basis. Unless you have or are living the lifestyle of most of these homeless women and children you just never know what is going on in the minds and hearts of each and every person who walk through the doors.  I have a 90% more positive  attitude and outlook on my life today than I did two years ago when I walked thru the lobby feeling broken, discouraged and unsure of the life I was struggling with.  I feel more encouraged about this L&F program who do more than just provide showers, a safety net, a warm temporary day shelter and hygiene kits. The love, smiles, positive mentoring and the gift of friendship and a sense of "belonging or acceptance".
Thank you all for being there for me.
With love... SLK :) <3<//Text>

<resp>None</resp>< Review>
After having my hair cut once or twice a month for the better part of 50 yrs., by professional barbers, this is the first time I've had someone charge an extra $5, atop the $15 price listed, because they had to "use scissors" (quote, unquote).
Perhaps they don't understand what a barber does? Or perhaps they need to change their name from the "Chop Shop' to what it appears to actually be... the "Clip Joint".
Two thumbs down for pegging my B.S. meter. It's a shame, too. They just lost a potential long term client.</Review>

<gmap_id>0x80dd32a9e9776c2f:0x1f8333cef241dbc7< /gmap_id><text>They call it an ADM (aka ADP)  fee. (Additional Dealer Markup fee)  It is basically a huge amount of money they do not advertise on the price of the vehicle. When you talk to them they brush over it quickly and hope you don't notice. They push you to come in to the dealer. It is completely unfounded and I personally run from any dealer that charges a markup fee or uses this tactic. I found to get the real price at a place like this you will most likely need to add at least 30 to 50 percent to the price they advertise. The formula I use is the price of the vehicle, plus tax, plus tag plus registration. Everything else should be included. ADM is a very frustrating and predatorial practice. Do not do business with dealers who do this. It is time to change the industry and put these greedy dishonest dealers out of business. Send a message the the dealers and manufacturers that we want the real price. If we pause purchasing, once bikes are sitting on their dealers floors for a few months, they will change quickly. Also look for other fees such as S&H, Shipping, Advertising, Dealer Prep or any uncapped fee.  For more info check out the article "10 fees you should never pay when buying a car" by Jack Sackman. (google it)<//text></record></dataset><record>

After a trip to the DMV and mentioning they still don't see it in their system a month after and one hour wait time with DMV on the 3rd month, finally got to the bottom of it. DMV stated something missing in the transfer application. No follow up with dealership even after multiple calls, I'm doing my own investigations.

This is the second bike I bought cash at moto united in the same year. First one from La Habra and no issue there. Will not be buying again at this location Moto United - Bellflower. Time spent calling the DMV when it should be the dealer is insane to go through. Nate was quick for a follow up call about the bike a week after purchase, just not on concerns with title or tags. So if I wanted to sell the bike, can't even do that 3 months after since paperwork from dealer hasn't been completed.

Dropping another 2 stars due to not still having tags or title after 90days. Temp registration is now expired and spoke to a law enforcement friend. It is now illegal to ride the bike and can be impounded if pulled over. Great, what to do since the ball is with the Moto United - Bellflower? If anyone else has this issue, open a case with CA AG for business complaint, if that doesn't work, I guess lawyer up for Breach of Vehicle Sale Contract.

Hopefully no one else runs into this issue. Frustrating when it's beyond your control or business does no follow up or shows concerns.

Update 1-19-2020

<name>Tiffany<//name>< Text>
I can't speak to the quality of the food, as this post is primarily in regards to this establishment's service and treatment of is guests. I visited the restaurant for brunch with my boyfriend on Superbowl Sunday earlier this year, and - although the restaurant was a bit full - we were seated by the host within a couple of minutes after checking in. Once they seated us, one of the bussers came to offer us water, and after that, everything went downhill. We were literally *never* approached by a waiter to come take our orders (despite repeated attempts to get the staff's attention), and we had started there waiting to be seen at our table for over 40 minutes. They even seated a party next to us (same two-person size), took their orders, and had them served before we finally were so fed up with their clearly intentional avoidance that we left. During the entire time we were patiently waiting to be attended to, we noticed that other tables that had been served had issues with either the bill they were charged or the food they had received (some combination of wrong orders and unsatisfying food quality). The only reason I can think of as to why they never served us is that we were the only patrons of color in the entire restaurant at that time, and I truly felt like we were being singled out for it as if I had gone back in time to the civil rights era. Maybe the food is good, but the terrible, seemingly discriminatory service really should be reason enough not to come here. I would not recommend to anyone who values their time or being treated with respect, and would never return on principle. Even if the issue was just one incompetent employee that was ill- equipped to do his job, I fault management as well for allowing this kind of behavior and poor, inconsistent customer service standards along its employees.<//Text>

<text>Highly recommended for date night or birthday!

Great location, fantastic drink selection, and the food really hits the spot. The staff is friendly and attentive, albeit a little overwhelmed. I stopped by for the Taco Tuesday and the tacos did not disappoint. The portions are generous, the meat is cooked perfectly, and each has their unique flavor with assorted toppings (al pastor came with fresh pineapple cubes!). The side salad with vinaigrette was a bit underwhelming though the tomatoes were very fresh. A side of french fries rounded out the meal, not over seasoned and hot out of the kitchen. Of drinks I recommend their signature Rye Tai, a craft beer from their selection (I'll take Allagash or Artifex), or a Pacifico with lime to make Taco Tuesday complete.

This restaurant's location is almost unbeatable. Located at the bottom of Del Mar right across the street from the San Clemente Pier. With shops and tourist traps surrounding the Pierside patio you'll get a bird's eye view of activity at one of the most popular destinations in southern California, not to mention a breathtaking view of the sunset behind the island offshore.

Food: 9/10
Drink: 10/10
Environment: 10/10
Staff: 9/10<//text><userid>118063098615605409784<//userid>< Gmap_id>

<Rating>1<//Rating><Review>I had the single worst restaurant experience of my life at this restaurant. It was so bad it resulted in me calling the police.

We called ahead and asked if we needed a reservation around noon. We were meeting my mother for her 65th birthday in San Clemente, and chose this restaurant because it had a patio that allowed dogs. We were told we did not need a reservation.

My wife, mother, and I arrived at about 1:30, and were told by a young hostess that we would need to wait. So we ordered drinks and waited for an hour. The hostess never said anything to us during this time. We never informed that we could sit inside with our dog. We were left alone to sit for an hour.

At the end of the hour, I went inside to check our table, at which point we were told that we couldn't eat there anymore because the kitchen was closed. This was clearly a huge error on the part of Pierside. We asked to talk to the manager, at which point Owner/Manager Keon Nayebdadash appeared to talk to us.

Instead of apologizing profusely for their error and their miscommunication, he became visibly furious and got in our faces (yes, including my fiance and 65 year old mother). This is a huge man, yelling at us and asking us if we "want to take it outside." My mom explained that it was her birthday and he said, "I don't care about the context," in her face. One of his employees said, "You better watch out, he knows the police!" It was the most shocking and incredible experience I have had in years.

We left the restaurant and retreated to a cheap pizza joint down the street where we had my mother's 65th Birthday meal. We called the police because we were so rattled, but they were not able to do anything.

< review>
If you could bring a C+ to life, Pierside would be it's physical form.
They have entr√©es they CAN charge more for, but they execute them with the bland beckiness of a Sysco delivery truck. The fish is frozen as are the hamburger patties...they taste fine and all but it's no secret to your tongue. The "wasabi" soba noodles under the ahi might as well be tossed in mayo... If that's not already what they do.
The one drink I had was the weekly special... a dragon fruit tequila cocktail which sounded great... But like the soba noodles... Tasted uninspired and fell flat.
It makes me wonder if the whole point is to keep from scaring away the local Beckies with too much flavor in fear of being labeled "ethnic"

Server was kind though. Loved her.<//review>

Filet  and wine.?

Pierside is home.  Welcome back.

< user_name>
Jordan Dunn<//user_name>
<Time>1581735200267< /Time>< review>
Firstly I must say, probably the best customer service experience I've had in my entire life. A short interaction that definitely made an impression.
I was recommended by a coworker to give Pippys a try, and I'm very glad I did. Placed my order online, which was quick and easy.
First thing I noticed, was the very affordable prices, paid $20 for an XL pepperoni pizza and 6pc wing, And that was including tip. In 25 min my order was ready for pickup. Arrived to a gentleman on the phone and he politely acknowledged me and I waited patiently. As soon as he finished his phone order, he promptly greeted me with a smile and a genuine sense of pride in the establishment(which was spotless, organized and very cozy).
He brought my order, reviewed my items for accuracy and handed them over. He proceeded to wish me a happy valentines day for myself and my family, and wished me a safe drive home.
When I arrived home, my family and I proceeded to enjoy a very well made pizza. Crispy crust on the outside and soft on the inside, taste was very fresh, flavor was very nice. I've seen some reviews complaining of plain crust, which I do not see as a negative trait.  Most pizza places treat the crust like garlic bread,  and I find it refreshing when a crust can be enjoyable with no added flavors or ingredients. My only suggestion is a little lighter on the seasoning on the pizza itself, a little strong. But overall this pizza was and is now in my top three local pizzas, only rival to San Biagios in Upland, and Black Market brewery in Temecula.
Next is my favorite food, the chicken wings, which I usually critique pretty strongly at establishments. And WOW,fresh tasting chicken, perfectly crispy, tossed in a well balanced buffalo sauce that's not over spicy, or overly sweet. Meaty flats, and substantial drums. To this point, Idyllwild Brew pub had my favorite local wings, and Pippys has now taken that spot over. Superb wings.

Overall, my experience was excellent, and I will absolutely return again. But the star of the show was the short and amazing customer service experience that I encountered.
This is a small local place that is quickly building a reputation, and I suggest if you've had a bad experience here, to give it another go as it's always better to give a second chance to a local establishment with heart, than a multimillion dollar chain that seldom cares about its customers. For the same price as a major chain, you can get a higher quality meal, and will help support a local gem. Keep it up guys< /review>
